\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02131}02131\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{Type\ unpack\ operator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02132}02132\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02133}02133\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{The\ type\ unpack\ operator\ takes\ the\ child\ types\ from\ some\ container\ type,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02134}02134\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{such\ as\ \`{}tuple[int,\ str]\`{}\ or\ a\ \`{}TypeVarTuple\`{},\ and\ 'pulls\ them\ out'.\ For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02135}02135\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02136}02136\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02137}02137\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \#\ For\ some\ generic\ class\ \`{}Foo\`{}:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02138}02138\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ Foo[Unpack[tuple[int,\ str]]]\ \ \#\ Equivalent\ to\ Foo[int,\ str]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02139}02139\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02140}02140\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ Ts\ =\ TypeVarTuple('Ts')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02141}02141\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \#\ Specifies\ that\ \`{}Bar\`{}\ is\ generic\ in\ an\ arbitrary\ number\ of\ types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02142}02142\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \#\ (Think\ of\ \`{}Ts\`{}\ as\ a\ tuple\ of\ an\ arbitrary\ number\ of\ individual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02143}02143\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \#\ \ \`{}TypeVar\`{}s,\ which\ the\ \`{}Unpack\`{}\ is\ 'pulling\ out'\ directly\ into\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02144}02144\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \#\ \ \`{}Generic[]\`{}.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02145}02145\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ class\ Bar(Generic[Unpack[Ts]]):\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02146}02146\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ Bar[int]\ \ \#\ Valid}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02149}02149\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{From\ Python\ 3.11,\ this\ can\ also\ be\ done\ using\ the\ \`{}*\`{}\ operator:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02236}02236\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ In\ the\ same\ way\ that\ a\ normal\ type\ variable\ is\ a\ stand-\/in\ for\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02237}02237\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ type\ such\ as\ \`{}\`{}int\`{}\`{},\ a\ type\ variable\ *tuple*\ is\ a\ stand-\/in\ for\ a\ *tuple*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02241}02241\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Consider\ the\ following\ example::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02242}02242\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02244}02244\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02245}02245\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ \`{}\`{}Ts\`{}\`{}\ type\ variable\ tuple\ here\ behaves\ like\ \`{}\`{}tuple[T1,\ T2]\`{}\`{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02246}02246\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ where\ \`{}\`{}T1\`{}\`{}\ and\ \`{}\`{}T2\`{}\`{}\ are\ type\ variables.\ To\ use\ these\ type\ variables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02247}02247\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ as\ type\ parameters\ of\ \`{}\`{}Array\`{}\`{},\ we\ must\ *unpack*\ the\ type\ variable\ tuple\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02248}02248\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ star\ operator:\ \`{}\`{}*Ts\`{}\`{}.\ The\ signature\ of\ \`{}\`{}Array\`{}\`{}\ then\ behaves}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02249}02249\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ as\ if\ we\ had\ simply\ written\ \`{}\`{}class\ Array(Generic[T1,\ T2]):\ ...\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02250}02250\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ In\ contrast\ to\ \`{}\`{}Generic[T1,\ T2]\`{}\`{},\ however,\ \`{}\`{}Generic[*Shape]\`{}\`{}\ allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{typing__extensions_8py_source_l02251}02251\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ us\ to\ parameterise\ the\ class\ with\ an\ *arbitrary*\ number\ of\ type\ parameters.}}
